##################################################

# STRATEGIC EFFECTS - A.K.A. "TRIGGERED MODIFIERS"
#
##################################################

# tentative defensive modifier
defend_minor = {
	potential = {
		is_ruler = yes
	}
	trigger = {
		any_war = {
			defender = {
				character = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	
	icon = 13
	
	general_opinion = 10
	city_vassal_min_levy = 0.15
	#city_vassal_max_levy = 0.1
	castle_vassal_min_levy = 0.15
	#castle_vassal_max_levy = 0.1
	temple_vassal_min_levy = 0.15
	#temple_vassal_max_levy = 0.1
	land_morale = 0.1
	land_organisation = 0.1
	city_vassal_tax_modifier = 0.1
	castle_vassal_tax_modifier = 0.1
	temple_vassal_tax_modifier = 0.1
	monthly_character_prestige = 1
}

# tentative offensive modifier
attack_unjust = {
	potential = {
		is_ruler = yes
	}
	trigger = {
		any_war = {
			attacker = {
				character = ROOT
			}	
		}	
	}
	
	icon = 31
	
	general_opinion = -10
	city_vassal_tax_modifier = -0.15
	castle_vassal_tax_modifier = -0.15
	temple_vassal_tax_modifier = -0.15
	#land_morale = -0.15
	#land_organisation = -0.05
	global_revolt_risk = 0.1
	monthly_character_prestige = -1
	build_time_modifier = 0.25
}

###LIBERT3 v11 Revamped Weakness Modifiers: All weakness-maluses revamped to be universal and have an authority (ie. prestige) malus (aside from the negative authority penalty itself), but only trigger for very pitiful rulers (4-)

### Scaled Modifiers ###
# Bankruptcy - Level 1
negative_finances = {
	potential = {
		is_ruler = yes
	}
	trigger = {
		wealth = -500
		NOT = { wealth = 0 }
	}
	
	icon = 24
	
	land_morale = -0.25
	monthly_character_prestige = -1
	general_opinion = -10
}
# Bankruptcy - Level 2
negative_finances = {
	potential = {
		is_ruler = yes
	}
	trigger = {
		wealth = -750
		NOT = { wealth = -500 }
	}
	
	icon = 24
	
	land_morale = -0.5
	monthly_character_prestige = -2
	general_opinion = -20
}

#Proof of Authority - Level 1
abundant_authority1 = {
	potential = {
		is_ruler = yes
	}
	trigger = {
		 prestige = 500 
		 NOT = { prestige = 1000 }
		 NOT = { trait = nomad }
		
	}
	
	icon = 7
	
	monthly_character_piety = 0.2
	#general_opinion = 10
	city_vassal_min_levy = 0.1
	city_vassal_max_levy = 0.1
	castle_vassal_min_levy = 0.1
	castle_vassal_max_levy = 0.1
	temple_vassal_min_levy = 0.1
	temple_vassal_max_levy = 0.1
	city_vassal_tax_modifier = 0.05
	castle_vassal_tax_modifier = 0.05
	temple_vassal_tax_modifier = 0.05
}

#Low decandence

		is_ruler = yes
	}

		religion_group = muslim
		NOT = { decadence = 10 }
	}
	icon = 17

	castle_vassal_max_levy = 0.1
	temple_vassal_max_levy = 0.1
	general_opinion = 15
	monthly_character_piety = 0.15
	monthly_character_prestige = 0.3
}

#Ruler Taking Command
ruler_command_yes = {
	potential = {
		age = 16
		is_ruler = yes	
		OR = {
			is_feudal = yes
			is_patrician = no
			is_theocracy = no
		}
	}	
	trigger = {		
		in_command = yes
		war = yes
	}
	icon = 1
	fertility = -0.5
	land_morale = 0.1
	land_organisation = 0.1
	monthly_character_prestige = 0.5
	general_opinion = 5
}

#Ruler Shirking Command
ruler_command_no = {
	potential = {
		age = 16
		is_ruler = yes	
		OR = {
			is_feudal = yes
			is_patrician = no
			is_theocracy = no
			is_councillor = no
		}
	}
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		war = yes
	}
	icon = 19
	monthly_character_prestige = -1
	general_opinion = -5
}

### Terrible Skills ###
#Diplomatic Disaster
weak_diplomacy = {
	potential = {
		is_feudal = yes
	}	
	trigger = {
		age = 16
		is_ruler = yes
		is_feudal = yes
		primary_title = { higher_tier_than = COUNT }
		NOT = { diplomacy = 5 }
	}
	
	icon = 21
	
	global_revolt_risk = 0.15
	general_opinion = -15
	monthly_character_prestige = -1.5
}

	general_opinion = 10

# Inspiring Leadership - 5 Pagan virtue traits out of 7 -> 21 combinations
paganleader5 = {
	potential = {
		is_ruler = yes
		NOT = { trait = incapable }
		OR = {
			religion = allfather
			religion = amanai
			religion = berber_pagan

	}
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			# Combination no 1
			AND = {
				trait = generous

				trait = proud
